Block dev servers outside tmux (exit 2 = blocked)\n    10→ *  2. Remind to use tmux for long-running commands (non-blocking)\n    11→ *  3. Block dev servers outside tmux\n    66→    if (process.platform !== 'win32' && !process.env.TMUX && DEV_SERVER.test(cmd)) {\n    67→      console.error('[Hook] BLOCKED: Dev server must run in tmux for log access');\n    68→      console.error('[Hook] Use: tmux new-session -d -s dev \"npm run dev\"');\n    69→      console.error('[Hook] Then: tmux attach -t dev');\n    70→      logHook('pre-bash-dispatch', 'Bash', cmd.slice(0, 60), 2, Date.now() - start);\n    71→      process.exit(2);\n    72→    }\n    73→\n    74→    // 2. Remind about tmux for long-running commands\n    75→    if (process.platform !== 'win32' && !process.env.TMUX && LONG_RUNNING.test(cmd)) {\n    76→      console.error('[Hook] Consider running in tmux for session persistence');\n    77→    }\n    78→\n    79→    // 3. Remind to review before git push\n    80→    if (/git push/.test(cmd)) {\n    81→      console.error('[Hook] Review changes before push...');\n    82→      console.error('[Hook] Continuing with push (remove this hook to add interactive review)');\n    83→    }\n    84→\n    85→    // 4. Secret guard: scan staged diff before git commit\n    86→    if (/\\bgit\\s+commit\\b/.test(cmd) && !cmd.includes('--no-verify')) {\n    87→      try {\n    88→        const diff = execFileSync('git', ['diff', '--staged', '--unified=0'], {\n    89→          encoding: 'utf8',\n    90→          timeout: 5000,\n    91→          stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'ignore'],\n    92→        });\n    93→        const secrets = scanForSecrets(diff);\n    94→        if (secrets.length > 0) {\n    95→          console.error('[Hook] SECRET GUARD — Potential secrets detected in staged changes:');\n    96→          for (const { type, snippet } of secrets) {\n    97→            console.error(`[Hook]   ${type}: ${snippet}`);\n    98→          }\n    99→          console.error('[Hook] Remove secrets and use environment variables instead.');\n   100→          console.error('[Hook] To bypass (only if this is a false positive): git commit --no-verify');\n   101→          logHook('pre-bash-dispatch', 'Bash', 'secret-guard-blocked', 2, Date.now() - start);\n   102→          process.exit(2);\n   103→        }\n   104→      } catch {\n   105→        // git not available, not a git repo, or timeout — pass through\n   106→      }\n   107→    }\n   108→  } catch {\n   109→    // Invalid input — pass through\n   110→  }\n   111→\n   112→  logHook('pre-bash-dispatch', 'Bash', cmd.slice(0, 60), 0, Date.now() - start);\n   113→  process.stdout.write(data);\n   114→  process.exit(0);\n   115→});\n   116→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. rawThreshold\n    29→    : 50;\n    30→\n    31→  let count = 1;\n    32→\n    33→  // Read existing count or start at 1\n    34→  // Use fd-based read+write to reduce (but not eliminate) race window\n    35→  // between concurrent hook invocations\n    36→  try {\n    37→    const fd = fs.openSync(counterFile, 'a+');\n    38→    try {\n    39→      const buf = Buffer.alloc(64);\n    40→      const bytesRead = fs.readSync(fd, buf, 0, 64, 0);\n    41→      if (bytesRead > 0) {\n    42→        const parsed = parseInt(buf.toString('utf8', 0, bytesRead).trim(), 10);\n    43→        // Clamp to reasonable range — corrupted files could contain huge values\n    44→        // that pass Number.isFinite() (e.g., parseInt('9'.repeat(30)) => 1e+29)\n    45→        count = (Number.isFinite(parsed) && parsed > 0 && parsed <= 1000000)\n    46→          ? parsed + 1\n    47→          : 1;\n    48→      }\n    49→      // Truncate and write new value\n    50→      fs.ftruncateSync(fd, 0);\n    51→      fs.writeSync(fd, String(count), 0);\n    52→    } finally {\n    53→      fs.closeSync(fd);\n    54→    }\n    55→  } catch {\n    56→    // Fallback: just use writeFile if fd operations fail\n    57→    writeFile(counterFile, String(count));\n    58→  }\n    59→\n    60→  // Suggest compact after threshold tool calls\n    61→  if (count === threshold) {\n    62→    log(`[StrategicCompact] ${threshold} tool calls reached - consider /compact if transitioning phases`);\n    63→  }\n    64→\n    65→  // Suggest at regular intervals after threshold (every 25 calls from threshold)\n    66→  if (count > threshold && (count - threshold) % 25 === 0) {\n    67→    log(`[StrategicCompact] ${count} tool calls - good checkpoint for /compact if context is stale`);\n    68→  }\n    69→\n    70→  process.exit(0);\n    71→}\n    72→\n    73→main().catch(err => {\n    74→  console.error('[StrategicCompact] Error:', err.message);\n    75→  process.exit(0);\n    76→});\n    77→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. The snapshot is appended to the active\n    10→ * session .tmp file so it survives compaction and is available to the\n    11→ * next SessionStart hook.\n    12→ *\n    13→ * Input (stdin JSON):\n    14→ *   { session_id, transcript_path, hook_event_name }\n    15→ */\n    16→\n    17→import fs from 'fs';\n    18→import path from 'path';\n    19→import { getSessionsDir, getDateTimeString, getTimeString, findFiles, ensureDir, appendFile, log } from '../lib/utils.js';\n    20→\n    21→const MAX_STDIN = 256 * 1024;\n    22→let data = '';\n    23→process.stdin.setEncoding('utf8');\n    24→process.stdin.on('data', chunk => {\n    25→  if (data.length < MAX_STDIN) data += chunk.substring(0, MAX_STDIN - data.length);\n    26→});\n    27→\n    28→/**\n    29→ * Extract a compact state snapshot from the JSONL transcript.\n    30→ * Returns an object with { taskLines, recentExchanges, filesMentioned }.\n    31→ */\n    32→function extractSnapshot(transcriptPath) {\n    33→  const snapshot = { taskLines: [], recentExchanges: [], filesMentioned: new Set() };\n    34→\n    35→  let raw;\n    36→  try {\n    37→    raw = fs.readFileSync(transcriptPath, 'utf8');\n    38→  } catch {\n    39→    return snapshot;\n    40→  }\n    41→\n    42→  const lines = raw.trim().split('\\n').filter(Boolean);\n    43→  const messages = [];\n    44→  for (const line of lines) {\n    45→    try {\n    46→      messages.push(JSON.parse(line));\n    47→    } catch {\n    48→      /* skip */\n    49→    }\n    50→  }\n    51→\n    52→  // Scan all messages for todo-like patterns and file paths\n    53→  const todoRe = /\\[([ xX])\\]\\s+(.+)/g;\n    54→  const fileRe = /(?:^|\\s)((?:\\/[\\w.-]+){2,}\\.[\\w]+)/g;\n    55→\n    56→  for (const msg of messages) {\n    57→    const text =\n    58→      typeof msg.content === 'string'\n    59→        ? msg.content\n    60→        : Array.isArray(msg.content)\n    61→          ? msg.content\n    62→              .filter(b => b.type === 'text')\n    63→              .map(b => b.text)\n    64→              .join(' ')\n    65→          : '';\n    66→\n    67→    for (const m of text.matchAll(todoRe)) {\n    68→      snapshot.taskLines.push(`[${m[1]}] ${m[2].slice(0, 120)}`);\n    69→    }\n    70→    for (const m of text.matchAll(fileRe)) {\n    71→      if (m[1].length < 200) snapshot.filesMentioned.add(m[1]);\n    72→    }\n    73→  }\n    74→\n    75→  // Grab last 6 user/assistant turns for recency context\n    76→  const turns = messages.filter(m => m.role === 'user' || m.role === 'assistant');\n    77→  const recent = turns.slice(-6);\n    78→  for (const t of recent) {\n    79→    const text =\n    80→      typeof t.content === 'string'\n    81→        ? t.content\n    82→        : Array.isArray(t.content)\n    83→          ? t.content\n    84→              .filter(b => b.type === 'text')\n    85→              .map(b => b.text)\n    86→              .join(' ')\n    87→          : '';\n    88→    if (text.trim()) {\n    89→      snapshot.recentExchanges.push(`[${t.role}] ${text.trim().slice(0, 200)}`);\n    90→    }\n    91→  }\n    92→\n    93→  return snapshot;\n    94→}\n    95→\n    96→process.stdin.on('end', () => {\n    97→  try {\n    98→    const sessionsDir = getSessionsDir();\n    99→    ensureDir(sessionsDir);\n   100→\n   101→    let sessionId = null;\n   102→ Injects at most 3000 characters to avoid\n    10→ * burning context on stale information from other projects.\n    11→ */\n    12→\n    13→import { spawnSync } from 'child_process';\n    14→import fs detectProjectType } from '../lib/project-detect.js';\n    21→\n    22→/**\n    23→ * Maps detected languages and frameworks to relevant clarc skills.\n    24→ * Used to surface skill recommendations at session start.\n    25→ */\n    26→const SKILL_MAP = {\n    27→  // Languages\n    28→  typescript: ['typescript-patterns', 'typescript-patterns-advanced', 'typescript-coding-standards'],\n    29→  javascript: ['typescript-coding-standards', 'async-patterns'],\n    30→  python: ['python-patterns', 'python-patterns-advanced', 'python-testing'],\n    31→  golang: ['go-patterns', 'cpp-patterns-advanced', 'cpp-testing'],\n    38→  // Frameworks\n    39→  react: ['state-management', 'frontend-patterns', 'e2e-testing'],\n    40→  nextjs: ['state-management', 'frontend-patterns', 'e2e-testing'],\n    41→  vue: ['state-management', 'frontend-patterns'],\n    42→  angular: ['state-management', 'frontend-patterns'],\n    43→  django: ['django-patterns', 'django-security', 'springboot-security', 'springboot-tdd'],\n    47→  rails: ['ruby-patterns', 'ruby-testing'],\n    48→  gin: ['go-patterns', 'go-testing'],\n    49→  echo: ['go-patterns', 'go-testing'],\n    50→ ['rust-patterns', 'rust-testing'],\n    54→  axum: ['rust-patterns', 'rust-testing']\n    55→};\n    56→\n    57→const MAX_INJECT_CHARS = 3000;\n    58→\n    59→// Stop words to ignore when extracting git-log keywords\n    60→const STOP_WORDS = new Set([\n    61→  'a',\n    62→  'an',\n    63→  'the',\n    64→  'and',\n    65→  'or',\n    66→  'but',\n    67→  'in',\n    68→  'on',\n    69→  'at',\n    70→  'to',\n    71→  'for',\n    72→  'of',\n    73→  'with',\n    74→  'by',\n    75→  'from',\n    76→  'up',\n    77→  'as',\n    78→  'is',\n    79→  'it',\n    80→  'its',\n    81→  'be',\n    82→  'are',\n    83→  'was',\n    84→  'were',\n    85→  'been',\n    86→  'has',\n    87→  'have',\n    88→  'had',\n    89→  'do',\n    90→  'does',\n    91→  'did',\n    92→  'will',\n    93→  'would',\n    94→  'could',\n    95→  'should',\n    96→  'may',\n    97→  'might',\n    98→  'shall',\n    99→  'can',\n   100→  'not',\n   101→  'no',\n   102→  'fix',\n   103→  'add',\n   104→  'update',\n   105→  'remove',\n   106→  'change',\n   107→  'use',\n   108→  'move',\n   109→  'make',\n   110→  'get',\n   111→  'set',\n   112→  'run',\n   113→  'feat',\n   114→  'chore',\n   115→  'docs',\n   116→  'test',\n   117→  'refactor',\n   118→  'perf',\n   119→  'ci'\n   120→]);\n   121→\n   122→/**\n   123→ * Extract meaningful keywords from recent git commit messages.\n   124→ * Returns a Set of lowercase tokens weighted by frequency (TF-style).\n   125→ * Falls back gracefully if git is unavailable.\n   126→ */\n   127→function extractGitKeywords(cwd, limit = 15) {\n   128→  try {\n   129→    const result = spawnSync('git', ['log', '--oneline', `-${limit}`], {\n   130→      cwd,\n   131→      stdio: 'pipe',\n   132→      encoding: 'utf8',\n   133→      timeout: 3000\n   134→    });\n   135→    if (result.status !== 0 || !result.stdout) return new Map();\n   136→\n   137→    const freq = new Map();\n   138→    for (const line of result.stdout.split('\\n')) {\n   139→      // Strip commit hash prefix\n   140→      const message = line.replace(/^[0-9a-f]+ /, '').toLowerCase();\n   141→      for (const token of message.split(/[\\s:/()\\-_,.[\\]{}'\"!?]+/)) {\n   142→        if (token.length < 3 || STOP_WORDS.has(token)) continue;\n   143→        freq.set(token, (freq.get(token) || 0) + 1);\n   144→      }\n   145→    }\n   146→    return freq;\n   147→  } catch {\n   148→    return new Map();\n   149→  }\n   150→}\n   151→\n   152→/**\n   153→ * Score a line by how many git-derived keywords it contains.\n   154→ * Weights higher-frequency keywords more (TF-style).\n   155→ */\n   156→function scoreLine(line, keywordFreq) {\n   157→  const lower = line.toLowerCase();\n   158→  let score = 0;\n   159→  for (const [token, freq] of keywordFreq) {\n   160→    if (lower.includes(token)) score += Math.log(1 + freq);\n   161→  }\n   162→  return score;\n   163→}\n   164→\n   165→/**\n   166→ * Filter session content to lines relevant to the current project.\n   167→ *\n   168→ * Strategy (in priority order):\n   169→ *  1. Lines that contain the project name (most specific signal)\n   170→ *  2. TF-IDF-style scoring using keywords from recent git commits\n   171→ *     (top-scored lines are more likely to be relevant to current work)\n   172→ *  3. Fall back to the last N lines (most recent context)\n   173→ *  4. Cap total output at MAX_INJECT_CHARS\n   174→ */\n   175→function filterSessionContent(content, projectName, cwd) {\n   176→  if (!content || content.includes('[Session context goes here]')) return null;\n   177→\n   178→  const lines = content.split('\\n');\n   179→\n   180→  // Always cap regardless of strategy\n   181→  const cap = text => (text.length > MAX_INJECT_CHARS ? '...(truncated)\\n' + text.slice(text.length - MAX_INJECT_CHARS) : text);\n   182→\n   183→  // Fast path: content is short enough to inject as-is\n   184→  if (content.length <= MAX_INJECT_CHARS) return content;\n   185→\n   186→  // Strategy 1: project-specific lines\n   187→  if (projectName) {\n   188→    const keyword = projectName.toLowerCase();\n   189→    const relevant = lines.filter(l => l.toLowerCase().includes(keyword));\n   190→    if (relevant.length >= 10) {\n   191→      return cap(relevant.join('\\n'));\n   192→    }\n   193→  }\n   194→\n   195→  // Strategy 2: TF-IDF scoring from recent git commit keywords\n   196→  const keywordFreq = extractGitKeywords(cwd || process.cwd());\n   197→  if (keywordFreq.size > 0) {\n   198→    const scored = lines\n   199→      .map((line, idx) => ({ line, idx, score: scoreLine(line, keywordFreq) }))\n   200→      .filter(({ score }) => score > 0)\n   201→      .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);\n   202→\n   203→    if (scored.length >= 5) {\n   204→      // Re-sort by original index to preserve narrative order\n   205→      const top = scored.slice(0, 60).sort((a, b) => a.idx - b.idx);\n   206→      return cap(top.map(({ line }) => line).join('\\n'));\n   207→    }\n   208→  }\n   209→\n   210→  // Strategy 3: keep the most recent lines (tail of the file)\n   211→  const tail = lines.slice(-150).join('\\n');\n   212→  return cap(tail);\n   213→}\n   214→\n   215→/**\n   216→ * Parse YAML frontmatter from a Rule markdown file.\n   217→ * Returns { globs, alwaysApply } or null if no frontmatter found.\n   218→ * Pure Node.js — no external dependencies.\n   219→ */\n   220→function parseRuleFrontmatter(content) {\n   221→  if (!content.startsWith('---')) return null;\n   222→  const end = content.indexOf('\\n---', 3);\n   223→  if (end === -1) return null;\n   224→  const yaml = content.slice(3, end);\n   225→  const globs = [];\n   226→  let alwaysApply = null;\n   227→\n   228→  for (const line of yaml.split('\\n')) {\n   229→    const trimmed = line.trim();\n   230→    // Parse \"globs:\" list items (- \"pattern\")\n   231→    const globMatch = trimmed.match(/^-\\s+\"?([^\"]+)\"?$/);\n   232→    if (globMatch) {\n   233→      globs.push(globMatch[1]);\n   234→    }\n   235→    if (trimmed.startsWith('alwaysApply:')) {\n   236→      alwaysApply = trimmed.includes('true');\n   237→    }\n   238→  }\n   239→\n   240→  return { globs, alwaysApply };\n   241→}\n   242→\n   243→/**\n   244→ * Simple glob matcher without external deps.\n   245→ * Converts glob patterns to regex and tests against file paths.\n   246→ * Supports * (any char except /), ** (any char incl /), ? (single char).\n   247→ */\n   248→function globMatches(pattern, filePath) {\n   249→  // Normalize slashes\n   250→  const p = filePath.replace(/\\\\/g, '/');\n   251→  // Convert glob to regex\n   252→  const regexStr = pattern\n   253→    .replace(/\\\\/g, '/')\n   254→    .replace(/\\./g, '\\\\.')\n   255→    .replace(/\\{([^}]+)\\}/g, (_, group) => `(${group.split(',').join('|')})`)\n   256→    .replace(/\\*\\*/g, '__GLOBSTAR__') // placeholder for ** before replacing *\n   257→    .replace(/\\*/g, '[^/]*')\n   258→    .replace(/__GLOBSTAR__/g, '.*')\n   259→    .replace(/\\?/g, '[^/]');\n   260→  try {\n   261→    return new RegExp(`(^|/)${regexStr}$`).test(p);\n   262→  } catch {\n   263→    return false;\n   264→  }\n   265→}\n   266→\n   267→/**\n   268→ * Scan installed Rules directories (~/.claude/rules/) for files with\n   269→ * globs frontmatter and check if any project files match.\n   270→ * Returns list of matched rule file paths (relative to rules dir).\n   271→ */\n   272→function detectGlobRules(cwd) {\n   273→  const claudeDir = path.join(os.homedir(), '.claude');\n   274→  const rulesDir = path.join(claudeDir, 'rules');\n   275→  if (!fs.existsSync(rulesDir)) return [];\n   276→\n   277→  // Collect project files via git ls-files (fast, respects .gitignore)\n   278→  let projectFiles = [];\n   279→  try {\n   280→    const r = spawnSync('git', ['ls-files'], { cwd, encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 5000 });\n   281→    if (r.status === 0 && r.stdout) {\n   282→      projectFiles = r.stdout.trim().split('\\n').filter(Boolean);\n   283→    }\n   284→  } catch {\n   285→    // Fallback: skip glob matching if git unavailable\n   286→    return [];\n   287→  }\n   288→\n   289→  if (projectFiles.length === 0) return [];\n   290→\n   291→  const matched = [];\n   292→\n   293→  // Walk all rule .md files\n   294→  function walkDir(dir, rel) {\n   295→    let entries;\n   296→    try {\n   297→      entries = fs.readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });\n   298→    } catch {\n   299→      return;\n   300→    }\n   301→    for (const entry of entries) {\n   302→      if (entry.isDirectory()) {\n   303→        walkDir(path.join(dir, entry.name), rel ? `${rel}/${entry.name}` : entry.name);\n   304→      } else if (entry.name.endsWith('.md')) {\n   305→        const filePath = path.join(dir, entry.name);\n   306→        const relPath = rel ? `${rel}/${entry.name}` : entry.name;\n   307→        const content = (() => {\n   308→          try {\n   309→            return fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');\n   310→          } catch {\n   311→            return '';\n   312→          }\n   313→        })();\n   314→        const meta = parseRuleFrontmatter(content);\n   315→        if (!meta) return;\n   316→\n   317→        // alwaysApply: true → skip (already loaded by Claude Code natively)\n   318→        if (meta.alwaysApply === true) return;\n   319→\n   320→        // No globs → skip\n   321→        if (meta.globs.length === 0) return;\n   322→\n   323→        // Check if any project file matches any glob\n   324→        const hit = meta.globs.some(glob => projectFiles.some(pf => globMatches(glob, pf)));\n   325→        if (hit) {\n   326→          matched.push(relPath);\n   327→        }\n   328→      }\n   329→    }\n   330→  }\n   331→\n   332→  walkDir(rulesDir, '');\n   333→  return matched;\n   334→}\n   335→\n   336→async function main() {\n   337→  const sessionsDir = getSessionsDir();\n   338→  const learnedDir = getLearnedSkillsDir();\n   339→\n   340→  // Ensure directories exist\n   341→  ensureDir(sessionsDir);\n   342→  ensureDir(learnedDir);\n   343→\n   344→  // Detect current project for relevance filtering\n   345→  const projectName = getProjectName ? getProjectName() : null;\n   346→\n   347→  // Check for recent session files (last 7 days)\n   348→  const recentSessions = findFiles(sessionsDir, '*-session.tmp', { maxAge: 7 });\n   349→\n   350→  if (recentSessions.length > 0) {\n   351→    const latest = recentSessions[0];\n   352→    log(`[SessionStart] Found ${recentSessions.length} recent session(s)`);\n   353→    log(`[SessionStart] Latest: ${latest.path}`);\n   354→\n   355→    const raw = readFile(latest.path);\n   356→    const filtered = filterSessionContent(raw, projectName, process.cwd());\n   357→    if (filtered) {\n   358→      const charCount = filtered.length;\n   359→      log(`[SessionStart] Injecting ${charCount} chars of session context (project: ${projectName || 'unknown'})`);\n   360→      output(`Previous session summary:\\n${filtered}`);\n   361→    }\n   362→  }\n   363→\n   364→  // Check for learned skills\n   365→  const learnedSkills = findFiles(learnedDir, '*.md');\n   366→\n   367→  if (learnedSkills.length > 0) {\n   368→    log(`[SessionStart] ${learnedSkills.length} learned skill(s) available in .clarc/ directory.\n   443→ * Reads brief.md + context.md + progress.md and injects as session context.\n   444→ * Falls back silently if .clarc/ does not exist.\n   445→ *\n   446→ * Priority: .clarc/ > session files (already loaded above)\n   447→ */\n   448→function loadMemoryBank(cwd) {\n   449→  const clarcDir = path.join(cwd, '.clarc');\n   450→  if (!fs.existsSync(clarcDir)) return;\n   451→\n   452→  const files = [\n   453→    { name: 'brief.md', label: 'Project Brief' },\n   454→    { name: 'context.md', label: 'Last Session Context' },\n   455→    { name: 'progress.md', label: 'Progress' },\n   456→  ];\n   457→\n   458→  const loaded = [];\n   459→  let combined = '';\n   460→\n   461→  for (const { name, label } of files) {\n   462→    const filePath = path.join(clarcDir, name);\n   463→    if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) continue;\n   464→    try {\n   465→      const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8').trim();\n   466→      if (!content) continue;\n   467→      // Cap each file at 2000 chars to avoid flooding context\n   468→      const capped = content.length > 2000 ? content.slice(0, 2000) + '\\n...(truncated)' : content;\n   469→      combined += `### ${label}\\n${capped}\\n\\n`;\n   470→      loaded.push(name);\n   471→    } catch {\n   472→      // Skip unreadable files\n   473→    }\n   474→  }\n   475→\n   476→  if (loaded.length > 0) {\n   477→    log(`[SessionStart] Memory Bank loaded: ${loaded.join(', ')}`);\n   478→    output(`--- Project Memory Bank ---\\n${combined.trim()}\\n---`);\n   479→  }\n   480→}\n   481→\n   482→/**\n   483→ * Parse simple YAML frontmatter (key: value pairs only) from a skill file.\n   484→ * Returns an object with any found keys; falls back to empty object.\n   485→ */\n   486→function parseSkillFrontmatter(content) {\n   487→  if (!content.startsWith('---')) return {};\n   488→  const end = content.indexOf('\\n---', 3);\n   489→  if (end === -1) return {};\n   490→  const yaml = content.slice(3, end);\n   491→  const result = {};\n   492→  for (const line of yaml.split('\\n')) {\n   493→    const m = line.match(/^(\\w[\\w-]*):\\s*(.+)$/);\n   494→    if (m) result[m[1]] = m[2].trim().replace(/^[\"']|[\"']$/g, '');\n   495→  }\n   496→  return result;\n   497→}\n   498→\n   499→/**\n   500→ * Scan .clarc/skills/ for project-local skill directories.\n   501→ * Each skill 'skills');\n   508→  if (!fs.existsSync(skillsDir)) return;\n   509→\n   510→  let entries;\n   511→  try {\n   512→    entries = fs.readdirSync(skillsDir, { withFileTypes: true });\n   513→  } catch 527→      content = fs.readFileSync(skillFile, 'utf8');\n   528→    } catch {\n   529→      continue;\n   530→    }\n   531→\n   532→    const meta = parseSkillFrontmatter(content);\n   533→    const title = meta.title || entry.name;\n   534→    const description = meta.description || '';\n   535→    const isOverride = Object.values(SKILL_MAP).flat().includes(entry.name);\n   536→\n   537→    if (isOverride) {\n   538→      overrides.push(entry.name);\n   539→      log(`[SessionStart] Local skill '${entry.name}' overrides global version`);\n   540→    }\n   541→\n   542→    found.push({ name: entry.name, title, description, isOverride });\n   543→  }\n   544→\n   545→  if (found.length === 0) return;\n   546→\n   547→  const names = found.map(s => `[local] ${s.name}${s.isOverride ? ' (overrides global)' : ''}`).join(', ');\n   548→  log(`[SessionStart] Project-local skills loaded: ${found.map(s => s.name).join(', ')}`);\n   549→  output(`Loaded ${found.length} project-local skill${found.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}: ${names}`);\n   550→}\n   551→\n   552→/**\n   553→ * Load agent instinct overlays from ~/.clarc/agent-instincts/.\n   554→ *\n   555→ * Each overlay file extends a specific agent with learned behaviors accumulated\n   556→ * via continuous-learning-v2. }\n   644→\n   645→  const daysSinceInstall = Math.floor((Date.now() - installMtime) / 86_400_000);\n   646→\n   647→  let upstreamVersion = null;\n   648→  try {\n   649→    if (fs.existsSync(upstreamVersionFile)) {\n   650→      upstreamVersion = fs.readFileSync(upstreamVersionFile, 'utf8').trim();\n   651→    }\n   652→  } catch { /* ignore */ }\n   653→\n   654→  const hasNewerVersion = upstreamVersion && upstreamVersion !== installedVersion;\n   655→  const isStale = daysSinceInstall > 30;\n   656→\n   657→  if (!hasNewerVersion && !isStale) return;\n   658→\n   659→  // Emit banner\n   660→  if (hasNewerVersion) {\n   661→    output(`Rules update available: v${installedVersion} → v${upstreamVersion}. Run /update-rules to get latest.`);\n   662→    log(`[SessionStart] Rules banner: update available ${installedVersion} → ${upstreamVersion}`);\n   663→  } else {\n   664→    output(`Rules last updated ${daysSinceInstall} days ago (v${installedVersion}).     1→#!/usr/bin/env node\n     2→/**\n     3→ * PostToolUse Hook — Auto-Checkpoint\n     4→ *\n     5→ * Creates a lightweight Git checkpoint after every Edit or Write tool call.\n     6→ * This lets users undo Claude's changes via the /undo command.\n     7→ *\n     8→ * Strategy:\n     9→ * - No initial commit in repo → git stash (reversible with git stash pop)\n    10→ * - Initial commit exists → fixup commit [skip ci] (reversible with git reset HEAD~1)\n    11→ * - Not in a Git repo → no-op, no error\n    12→ *\n    13→ * Rate limiting: max 1 checkpoint per 60 seconds (prevents spam).\n    14→ * Log: ~/.clarc/checkpoints.log (append-only, capped at 50 entries)\n    15→ */\n    16→\n    17→import { spawnSync } from 'child_process';\n    18→import fs from 'fs';\n    19→import path from 'path';\n    20→import os from 'os';\n    21→\n    22→const CHECKPOINT_INTERVAL_MS = 60_000; // 1 checkpoint per 60s max\n    23→const MAX_LOG_ENTRIES = 50;\n    24→const CLARC_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.clarc');\n    25→const LOG_FILE = path.join(CLARC_DIR, 'checkpoints.log');\n    26→\n    27→function log(msg) {\n    28→  process.stderr.write(`[AutoCheckpoint] ${msg}\\n`);\n    29→}\n    30→\n    31→function git(args, cwd) {\n    32→  return spawnSync('git', args, { cwd, encoding: 'utf8', stdio: 'pipe', timeout: 10_000 });\n    33→}\n    34→\n    35→function isGitRepo(cwd) {\n    36→  const r = git(['rev-parse', '--git-dir'], cwd);\n    37→  return r.status === 0;\n    38→}\n    39→\n    40→function hasInitialCommit(cwd) {\n    41→  const r = git(['rev-parse', 'HEAD'], cwd);\n    42→  return r.status === 0;\n    43→}\n    44→\n    45→function hasUnstagedChanges(cwd) {\n    46→  const r = git(['status', '--porcelain'], cwd);\n    47→  return r.status === 0 && r.stdout.trim().length > 0;\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→function ensureClarcDir() {\n    51→  if (!fs.existsSync(CLARC_DIR)) {\n    52→    fs.mkdirSync(CLARC_DIR, { recursive: true });\n    53→  }\n    54→}\n    55→\n    56→function readLog() {\n    57→  try {\n    58→    return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(LOG_FILE, 'utf8'));\n    59→  } catch {\n    60→    return [];\n    61→  }\n    62→}\n    63→\n    64→function writeLog(entries) {\n    65→  ensureClarcDir();\n    66→  // Cap at MAX_LOG_ENTRIES (keep newest)\n    67→  const capped = entries.slice(-MAX_LOG_ENTRIES);\n    68→  fs.writeFileSync(LOG_FILE, JSON.stringify(capped, null, 2), 'utf8');\n    69→}\n    70→\n    71→function appendLogEntry(entry) {\n    72→  const entries = readLog();\n    73→  entries.push(entry);\n    74→  writeLog(entries);\n    75→}\n    76→\n    77→function isRateLimited() {\n    78→  const entries = readLog();\n    79→  if (entries.length === 0) return false;\n    80→  const last = entries[entries.length - 1];\n    81→  return last && Date.now() - new Date(last.timestamp).getTime() < CHECKPOINT_INTERVAL_MS;\n    82→}\n    83→\n    84→// Read hook input from stdin\n    85→let stdinData = '';\n    86→process.stdin.setEncoding('utf8');\n    87→process.stdin.on('data', chunk => { stdinData += chunk; });\n    88→process.stdin.on('end', () => {\n    89→  main().catch(err => {\n    90→    log(`Error: ${err.message}`);\n    91→    process.exit(0);\n    92→  });\n    93→});\n    94→\n    95→async function main() {\n    96→  // Parse tool name from hook input\n    97→  let toolName = '';\n    98→  let toolInput = {};\n    99→  try {\n   100→    const input = JSON.parse(stdinData);\n   101→    toolName = input.tool_name || '';\n   102→    toolInput = input.tool_input || {};\n   103→  } catch {\n   104→    // Ignore parse errors — run anyway\n   105→  }\n   106→\n   107→  // Only act on Edit and Write tools\n   108→  if (toolName !== 'Edit' && toolName !== 'Write') {\n   109→    process.exit(0);\n   110→  }\n   111→\n   112→  const cwd = process.cwd();\n   113→\n   114→  if (!isGitRepo(cwd)) {\n   115→    log('Not a git repo — skipping checkpoint');\n   116→    process.exit(0);\n   117→  }\n   118→\n   119→  if (!hasUnstagedChanges(cwd)) {\n   120→    log('No changes to checkpoint');\n   121→    process.exit(0);\n   122→  }\n   123→\n   124→  if (isRateLimited()) {\n   125→    log('Rate limited — skipping checkpoint (< 60s since last)');\n   126→    process.exit(0);\n   127→  }\n   128→\n   129→  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();\n   130→  const filePath = toolInput.file_path || toolInput.path || 'unknown';\n   131→\n   132→  if (!hasInitialCommit(cwd)) {\n   133→    // Strategy: git stash\n   134→    63→function isCoolingDown(hookId, minutes = 5) {\n    64→  try {\n    65→    const cooldowns = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(COOLDOWN_PATH, 'utf8'));\n    66→    const last = cooldowns[hookId];\n    67→    if (last && (Date.now() - last) < minutes * 60 * 1000) return true;\n    68→  } catch { /* not found */ }\n    69→  return false;\n    70→}\n    71→\n    72→function setCooldown(hookId) {\n    73→  let cooldowns = {};\n    74→  try { cooldowns = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(COOLDOWN_PATH, 'utf8')); } catch { /* not found */ }\n    75→  cooldowns[hookId] = Date.now();\n    76→  try {\n    77→ Walks up from the file's\n     8→ * directory to find the nearest tsconfig.json, then runs tsc --noEmit\n     9→ * and reports only errors related to the edited file.\n    10→ */\n    11→\n    12→import { execFileSync } from 'child_process';\n    13→import fs from 'fs';\n    14→import path from 'path';\n    15→\n    16→const MAX_STDIN = 1024 * 1024; // 1MB limit\n    17→let data = \"\";\n 23→    data += chunk.substring(0, remaining);\n    24→  }\n    25→});\n    26→\n    27→process.stdin.on(\"end\", () => {\n    28→  try {\n    29→    const input = JSON.parse(data);\n    30→    const (!fs.existsSync(resolvedPath)) {\n    35→        process.stdout.write(data);\n    36→        process.exit(0);\n    37→      }\n    38→      // Find nearest tsconfig.json by walking up (max 20 levels to prevent infinite loop)\n    39→      let dir = path.dirname(resolvedPath);\n    40→      const root = path.parse(dir).root;\n    41→      let depth = 0;\n    42→\n    43→      while (dir !== root && depth < 20) {\n    44→        if (fs.existsSync(path.join(dir, \"tsconfig.json\"))) {\n    45→          break;\n    46→        }\n    47→        dir = path.dirname(dir);\n    48→        depth++;\n    49→      }\n    50→\n    51→      if (fs.existsSync(path.join(dir, \"tsconfig.json\"))) {\n    52→        try {\n    53→          // Use npx.cmd on Windows to avoid shell: true which enables command injection\n    54→          const npxBin = process.platform === \"win32\" ? \"npx.cmd\" : \"npx\";\n    55→          execFileSync(npxBin, [\"tsc\", \"--noEmit\", \"--pretty\", \"false\"], {\n    56→            cwd: dir,\n    57→            encoding: \"utf8\",\n    58→            stdio: [\"pipe\", \"pipe\", \"pipe\"],\n    59→            timeout: 30000,\n    60→          });\n    61→        } catch (err) {\n    62→          // tsc exits non-zero when there are errors — filter to edited file\n    63→          const output = (err.stdout || \"\") + (err.stderr || \"\");\n    64→          // Compute paths that uniquely identify the edited file.\n    65→          // tsc output uses paths relative to its cwd (the tsconfig dir),\n    66→          // so check for the relative path, absolute path, and original path.\n    67→          // Avoid bare basename matching — it causes false positives when\n    68→          // multiple files share the same name (e.g., src/utils.ts vs tests/utils.ts).\n    69→          const relPath = path.relative(dir, resolvedPath);\n    70→          const candidates = new Set([filePath, resolvedPath, relPath]);\n    71→          const relevantLines = output\n    72→            .split(\"\\n\")\n    73→            .filter((line) => {\n    74→              for (const candidate of candidates) {\n    75→                if (line.includes(candidate)) return true;\n    76→              }\n    77→              return false;\n    78→            })\n    79→            .slice(0, 10);\n    80→\n    81→          if (relevantLines.length > 0) {\n    82→ Extracts a meaningful summary from\n     8→ * the session transcript (via stdin JSON transcript_path) and saves it\n     9→ * to a session file for cross-session continuity.\n    10→ */\n    11→\n    12→import path from 'path';\n    13→import fs from 'fs';\n    14→import os from 'os';\n    15→import { getSessionsDir, getDateString, getTimeString, getSessionIdShort, ensureDir, readFile, writeFile, replaceInFile, log } from '../lib/utils.js';\n    16→\n    17→// Cost estimation constants (Claude Sonnet, 2026 pricing)\n    18→const SONNET_INPUT_USD_PER_M = 3.0;\n    19→const SONNET_OUTPUT_USD_PER_M = 15.0;\n    20→// Empirical heuristic: ~1200 input + ~300 output tokens per tool call on average\n    21→const EST_INPUT_TOKENS_PER_CALL = 1200;\n    22→const EST_OUTPUT_TOKENS_PER_CALL = 300;\n    23→\n    24→const CLARC_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.clarc');\n    25→const COST_LOG_FILE = path.join(CLARC_DIR, 'cost-log.jsonl');\n    26→\n    27→/**\n    28→ * Extract a meaningful summary from the session transcript.\n    29→ * Reads the JSONL transcript and pulls out key information:\n    30→ * - User messages (tasks requested)\n    31→ * - Tools used\n    32→ * - Files modified\n    33→ */\n    34→function extractSessionSummary(transcriptPath) {\n    35→  const content = readFile(transcriptPath);\n    36→  if (!content) return null;\n    37→\n    38→  const lines = content.split('\\n').filter(Boolean);\n    39→  const userMessages = [];\n    40→  const toolsUsed = new Set();\n    41→  const filesModified = new Set();\n    42→  let parseErrors = 0;\n    43→\n    44→  for (const line of lines) {\n    45→    try {\n    46→      const entry = JSON.parse(line);\n    47→\n    48→      // Collect user messages (first 200 chars each)\n    49→      if (entry.type === 'user' || entry.role === 'user' || entry.message?.role === 'user') {\n    50→        // Support both direct content and nested message.content (Claude Code JSONL format)\n    51→        const rawContent = entry.message?.content ?? entry.content;\n    52→        const text = typeof rawContent === 'string' ? rawContent : Array.isArray(rawContent) ? rawContent.map(c => (c && c.text) || '').join(' ') : '';\n    53→        if (text.trim()) {\n    54→          userMessages.push(text.trim().slice(0, 200));\n    55→        }\n    56→      }\n    57→\n    58→      // Collect tool names and modified files (direct tool_use entries)\n    59→      if (entry.type === 'tool_use' || entry.tool_name) {\n    60→        const toolName = entry.tool_name || entry.name || '';\n    61→        if (toolName) toolsUsed.add(toolName);\n    62→\n    63→        const filePath = entry.tool_input?.file_path || entry.input?.file_path || '';\n    64→        if (filePath && (toolName === 'Edit' || toolName === 'Write')) {\n    65→          filesModified.add(filePath);\n    66→        }\n    67→      }\n    68→\n    69→      // Extract tool uses from assistant message content blocks (Claude Code JSONL format)\n    70→      if (entry.type === 'assistant' && Array.isArray(entry.message?.content)) {\n    71→        for (const block of entry.message.content) {\n    72→          if (block.type === 'tool_use') {\n    73→            const toolName = block.name || '';\n    74→            if (toolName) toolsUsed.add(toolName);\n    75→\n    76→            const filePath = block.input?.file_path || '';\n    77→            if (filePath && (toolName === 'Edit' || toolName === 'Write')) {\n    78→              filesModified.add(filePath);\n    79→            }\n    80→          }\n    81→        }\n    82→      }\n    83→    } catch {\n    84→      parseErrors++;\n    85→    }\n    86→  }\n    87→\n    88→  if (parseErrors > 0) {\n    89→    log(`[SessionEnd] Skipped ${parseErrors}/${lines.length} unparseable transcript lines`);\n    90→  }\n    91→\n    92→  if (userMessages.length === 0) return null;\n    93→\n    94→  return {\n    95→    userMessages: userMessages.slice(-10), // Last 10 user messages\n    96→    toolsUsed: Array.from(toolsUsed).slice(0, 20),\n    97→    filesModified: Array.from(filesModified).slice(0, 30),\n    98→    totalMessages: userMessages.length\n    99→  };\n   100→}\n   101→\n   102→/**\n   103→ * Estimate session cost from tool call count and append to ~/.clarc/cost-log.jsonl.\n   104→ * Tool calls are the only reliable proxy we have without direct API access.\n   105→ * Disclaimer is always shown so users know this is an approximation.\n   106→ */\n   107→function logSessionCost(toolCallCount, sessionId, date) {\n   108→  try {\n   109→    if (toolCallCount === 0) return;\n   110→\n   111→    const estInputTokens = toolCallCount * EST_INPUT_TOKENS_PER_CALL;\n   112→    const estOutputTokens = toolCallCount * EST_OUTPUT_TOKENS_PER_CALL;\n   113→    const estUsd = (estInputTokens / 1_000_000) * SONNET_INPUT_USD_PER_M + (estOutputTokens / 1_000_000) * SONNET_OUTPUT_USD_PER_M;\n   114→\n   115→    const entry = {\n   116→      date,\n   117→      session_id: sessionId,\n   118→      tool_calls: toolCallCount,\n   119→      estimated_input_tokens: estInputTokens,\n   120→      estimated_output_tokens: estOutputTokens,\n   121→      estimated_usd: Math.round(estUsd * 10000) / 10000,\n   122→      project: path.basename(process.cwd()),\n   123→      disclaimer: 'Estimate only — exact costs at console.anthropic.com'\n   124→    };\n   125→\n   126→    if (!fs.existsSync(CLARC_DIR)) {\n   127→      fs.mkdirSync(CLARC_DIR, { recursive: true });\n   128→    }\n   129→    fs.appendFileSync(COST_LOG_FILE, JSON.stringify(entry) + '\\n', 'utf8');\n   130→\n   131→    const totalK = Math.round((estInputTokens + estOutputTokens) / 100) / 10;\n   132→    log(`[SessionEnd] Cost estimate: ${toolCallCount} tool calls | ~${totalK}k tokens | ~$${entry.estimated_usd.toFixed(4)} (Schätzung)`);\n   133→  } catch (err) {\n   134→    log(`[SessionEnd] Cost logging error: ${err.message}`);\n   135→  }\n   136→}\n   137→\n   138→// Read hook input from stdin (Claude Code provides transcript_path via stdin JSON)\n   139→const MAX_STDIN = 1024 * 1024;\n   140→let stdinData = '';\n   141→process.stdin.setEncoding('utf8');\n   142→\n   143→process.stdin.on('data', chunk => {\n   144→  if (stdinData.length < MAX_STDIN) {\n   145→    const remaining = MAX_STDIN - stdinData.length;\n   146→    stdinData += chunk.substring(0, remaining);\n   147→  }\n   148→});\n   149→\n   150→process.stdin.on('end', () => {\n   151→  runMain();\n   152→});\n   153→\n   154→function runMain() {\n   155→  main().catch(err => {\n   156→    console.error('[SessionEnd] Error:', err.message);\n   157→    process.exit(0);\n   158→  });\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→async function main() {\n   162→  // Parse stdin JSON to get transcript_path\n   163→  let transcriptPath = null;\n   164→  try {\n   165→    const input = JSON.parse(stdinData);\n   166→    transcriptPath = input.transcript_path;\n   167→  } catch {\n   168→    // Fallback: try env var for backwards compatibility\n   169→    transcriptPath = process.env.CLAUDE_TRANSCRIPT_PATH;\n   170→  }\n   171→\n   172→  const sessionsDir = getSessionsDir();\n   173→  const today = getDateString();\n   174→  const shortId = getSessionIdShort();\n   175→  const sessionFile = path.join(sessionsDir, `${today}-${shortId}-session.tmp`);\n   176→\n   177→  ensureDir(sessionsDir);\n   178→\n   179→  const currentTime = // Token/cost tracking\n   193→  const toolCallCount = summary ? summary.toolsUsed.length : 0;\n   194→  logSessionCost(toolCallCount, shortId, today);\n   195→\n   196→  // Context window warning: fires when session > 90min and .clarc/context.md is absent or stale\n   197→  checkContextWarning(sessionFile);\n   198→\n   199→  if (fs.existsSync(sessionFile)) {\n   200→    // Update existing end-of-string to avoid duplicate ### Stats sections\n   212→        const updatedContent = existing.replace(/## (?:Session Summary|Current State)[\\s\\S]*?$/, buildSummarySection(summary).trim() +    // Create new session file\n   220→    const summarySection = summary\n   221→      ? buildSummarySection(summary)\n   222→      : `## Current State\\n\\n[Session context goes here]\\n\\n### Completed\\n- [ ]\\n\\n### In Progress\\n- [ ]\\n\\n### Notes for Next Session\\n-\\n\\n### Context to Load\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n[relevant files]\\n\\`\\`\\``;\n   223→\n   224→    const template = `#  234→    writeFile(sessionFile, template);\n   235→    log(`[SessionEnd] Created session file: ${sessionFile}`);\n   236→  }\n   237→\n   238→  // Weekly Evolve-Batch: trigger on Mondays when >= 10   251→ * Only runs when .clarc/ already exists in the current working directory —\n   252→ * never creates .clarc/ automatically (user must opt in).\n   253→ */\n   254→function writeMemoryBank(summary, date, time) {\n   255→  const projectRoot = process.env.CLARC_PROJECT_ROOT || process.cwd();\n   256→  const clarcDir = path.join(projectRoot, '.clarc');\n   257→  if (!fs.existsSync(clarcDir)) {\n   258→    // Hint if project-like directory (has package.json, go.mod, etc.)\n   259→    const markers = ['package.json', 'go.mod', 'Cargo.toml', 'pyproject.toml', 'build.gradle'];\n   260→    const isProject = markers.some(m => fs.existsSync(path.join(projectRoot, m)));\n   261→    if (isProject) {\n   262→      log('[SessionEnd] Tip: create .clarc/ to enable Memory Bank (see docs/memory-bank.md)');\n   263→    }\n   264→    return;\n   265→  }\n   266→\n   267→  try {\n   268→    // Overwrite context.md with current session summary\n   269→    const window: keep last 30 sessions)\n   273→    const progressEntry = buildProgressEntry(summary, date, time);\n   274→    const progressFile = path.join(clarcDir, 'progress.md');\n   275→    const HEADER = '# Session Progress Log\\n\\n';\n   276→    const MAX_SESSIONS = 30;\n   277→\n   278→    let existing = fs.existsSync(progressFile) ? fs.readFileSync(progressFile, 'utf8') : HEADER;\n   279→    // Strip header for processing\n   280→    const body = existing.startsWith(HEADER) ? existing.slice(HEADER.length) : existing;\n   281→    // Split into individual session blocks (each starts with \"## Session \")\n   282→    const blocks = body.split(/(?=^## Session )/m).filter(Boolean);\n   283→    // Keep last MAX_SESSIONS - 1 to make room for the new entry\n   284→    const trimmed = blocks.slice(-(MAX_SESSIONS - 1));\n   285→    fs.writeFileSync(progressFile, HEADER + trimmed.join('') + progressEntry, 'utf8');\n   286→\n   287→    log(`[SessionEnd] Memory Bank updated: .clarc/context.md, .clarc/progress.md`);\n   288→  } catch (err) {\n   289→    log(`[SessionEnd] Memory Bank write error: ${err.message}`);\n   290→  }\n   291→}\n   292→\n   293→function buildContextFile(summary, date) {\n   294→  const tasks = summary.userMessages\n   295→    .slice(-5)\n   296→    .map(m => `- ${m.replace(/\\n/g, ' ').slice(0, 120)}`)\n   297→    .join('\\n');\n   298→\n   299→  const files = summary.filesModified.length > 0\n   300→    ? summary.filesModified.slice(0, 10).map(f => `- ${f}`).join('\\n')\n   301→    : '- (none)';\n   302→\n   303→  return `# Session Context — ${date}\n   304→\n   305→## Current focus\n   306→${tasks || '- (no tasks captured)'}\n   307→\n   308→## Files changed this session\n   309→${files}\n   310→\n   311→## Open TODOs\n   312→- [ ] (review and update manually)\n   313→\n   314→## Next steps\n   315→(update manually after reviewing session)\n   316→`;\n   317→}\n   318→\n   319→function buildProgressEntry(summary, date, time) {\n   320→  const tasks = summary.userMessages\n   321→    .slice(-5)\n   322→    .map(m => `  - ${m.replace(/\\n/g, ' ').slice(0, 120)}`)\n   323→    .join('\\n');\n   324→\n   325→ 10 instincts exist.\n   345→ */\n   346→function checkWeeklyEvolve() {\n   347→  try {\n   348→    const today = new Date();\n   349→    if (today.getDay() !== 1) return; // Only on Mondays\n   350→\n   351→    const claudeDir = process.env.CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT || path.join(os.homedir(), '.claude');\n   352→    const homunculusDir = path.join(claudeDir, 'homunculus');\n   353→    const lastEvolveFile sixDaysAgo = Date.now() - 6 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n   365→    if (lastEvolveDate && lastEvolveDate.getTime() > sixDaysAgo) return;\n   366→\n   367→    // Count instincts — stop as soon as threshold is reached\n   368→    const THRESHOLD = 10;\n   369→    let instinctCount = 0;\n   370→    outer: if (fs.existsSync(homunculusDir)) {\n   371→      for (const entry of fs.readdirSync(homunculusDir)) {\n   372→        if (entry.endsWith('.json') && entry !== 'last-evolve.json') {\n   373→          if (++instinctCount >= THRESHOLD) break outer;\n   374→        }\n   375→      }\n   376→      const 382→              if ((f.endsWith('.yaml') || f.endsWith('.json')) && ++instinctCount >= THRESHOLD) break outer;\n   383→            }\n   384→          }\n   385→        }\n   386→      }\n   387→    }\n   388→\n   389→    if (instinctCount < THRESHOLD) return;\n   390→\n   391→    // Write weekly evolve suggestion to notification queue\n   392→    const digestDir = path.join(homunculusDir);\n   393→    ensureDir(digestDir);\n   394→    const digestFile = path.join(digestDir, 'weekly-digest.md');\n   395→    const dateStr = today.toISOString().slice(0, 10);\n   396→\n   397→    const content Run /evolve to review.`);\n   414→  } catch (err) {\n   415→    log(`[SessionEnd] Weekly evolve check error: ${err.message}`);\n   416→  }\n   417→}\n   418→\n   419→/**\n   420→ * Warn when session > 90 minutes and .clarc/context.md is absent or stale (> 60 min old).\n   421→ * The warning is written to the session file and logged — it is NOT blocking.\n   422→ */\n   423→function checkContextWarning(sessionFile) {\n   424→  try {\n   425→    const NINETY_MINUTES_MS = 90 * 60 * 1000;\n   426→    const SIXTY_MINUTES_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000;\n   427→\n   428→    // Determine session start time from the session file mtime (creation time proxy)\n   429→    if (!fs.existsSync(sessionFile)) return;\n   430→    const sessionStat = fs.statSync(sessionFile);\n   431→    const sessionAgeMs = Date.now() - sessionStat.birthtimeMs;\n   432→\n   433→    if (sessionAgeMs < NINETY_MINUTES_MS) return; // session < 90 min, no warning needed\n   434→\n   435→    // Check .clarc/context.md in cwd\n   436→    const clarcDir = path.join(process.cwd(), '.clarc');\n   437→    const contextFile = path.join(clarcDir, 'context.md');\n   438→\n   439→    let contextStale = true;\n   440→    if (fs.existsSync(contextFile)) {\n   441→      const contextStat = fs.statSync(contextFile);\n   442→      const contextAgeMs = Date.now() - contextStat.mtimeMs;\n   443→      contextStale = contextAgeMs > SIXTY_MINUTES_MS;\n   444→    }\n   445→\n   446→    if (!contextStale) return; // context.md is fresh, no warning needed\n   447→\n   448→    const hasClarcDir = fs.existsSync(clarcDir);\n   449→    const hint = hasClarcDir\n   450→      ? 'Run /checkpoint create to save context before /compact.'\n   451→      : 'Create .clarc/ to enable Memory Bank: mkdir .clarc';\n   452→\n   453→    log(`[SessionEnd] ⚠ Long session (${Math.round(sessionAgeMs / 60000)}min) without recent context checkpoint. ${hint}`);\n   454→  } catch (err) {\n   455→    log(`[SessionEnd] Context warning check error: ${err.message}`);\n   456→  }\n   457→}\n   458→\n   459→function buildSummarySection(summary) {\n   460→  let section = '## Session Summary\\n\\n';\n   461→\n   462→  // Tasks (from user messages — collapse newlines and escape backticks to prevent markdown breaks)\n   463→  section += '### Tasks\\n';\n   464→  for (const msg of summary.userMessages) {\n   465→    section += `- ${msg.replace(/\\n/g, ' ').replace(/`/g, '\\\\`')}\\n`;\n   466→  }\n   467→  section += '\\n';\n   468→\n   469→  // Files modified\n   470→  if (summary.filesModified.length > 0) {\n   471→    section += '### Files Modified\\n';\n   472→    for (const f of summary.filesModified) {\n   473→      section += `- ${f}\\n`;\n   474→    }\n   475→    section += '\\n';\n   476→  }\n   477→\n   478→  // Tools used\n   479→  if (summary.toolsUsed.length > 0) {\n   480→    section += `### Tools Used\\n${summary.toolsUsed.join(', ')}\\n\\n`;\n   481→  }\n   482→\n   483→  section += `### Stats\\n- Total user messages: ${summary.totalMessages}\\n`;\n   484→\n   485→  return section;\n   486→}\n   487→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // last 7 days\n    53→\n    54→  // Scan instincts from ~/.claude/homunculus/\n    55→  const homunculusDir = path.join(claudeDir, 'homunculus');\n    56→  if (fs.existsSync(homunculusDir)) {\n    57→    const instincts = [];\n    58→    for (const entry of fs.readdirSync(homunculusDir)) {\n    59→      if (!entry.endsWith('.json')) continue;\n    60→      try {\n    61→        const fpath = path.join(homunculusDir, entry);\n    62→        const stat = fs.statSync(fpath);\n    63→        if (stat.mtimeMs < cutoff) continue;\n    64→        const obj = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(fpath, 'utf8'));\n    65→        const desc = obj.description || obj.pattern || obj.instinct || entry.replace('.json', '');\n    66→        const conf = obj.confidence !== null && obj.confidence !== undefined ? ` (conf: ${obj.confidence})` : '';\n    67→        instincts.push(`  • ${String(desc).slice(0, 100)}${conf}`);\n    68→      } catch {\n    69→        /* skip malformed */\n    70→      }\n    71→    }\n    72→    if (instincts.length > 0) {\n    73→      lines.push(`**Instincts learned this week (${instincts.length}):**`);\n    74→      lines.push(...instincts.slice(0, 10));\n    75→      if (instincts.length > 10) lines.push(`  …and ${instincts.length - 10} more`);\n    76→    }\n    77→  }\n    78→\n    79→  // Scan skills from ~/.claude/skills/learned/\n    80→  const learnedDir = path.join(claudeDir, 'skills', 'learned');\n    81→  if (fs.existsSync(learnedDir)) {\n    82→    const skills = [];\n    83→    for (const entry of fs.readdirSync(learnedDir)) {\n    84→      try {\n    85→        const fpath = path.join(learnedDir, entry);\n    86→        if (!fs.statSync(fpath).isDirectory()) continue;\n    87→        const skillFile = path.join(fpath, 'SKILL.md');\n    88→        if (!fs.existsSync(skillFile)) continue;\n    89→        const stat = fs.statSync(skillFile);\n    90→        if (stat.mtimeMs < cutoff) continue;\n    91→        skills.push(`  • ${entry}`);\n    92→      } catch {\n    93→        /* skip */\n    94→      }\n    95→    }\n    96→    if (skills.length > 0) {\n    97→      if (lines.length > 0) lines.push('');\n    98→      lines.push(`**Skills extracted this week (${skills.length}):**`);\n    99→      lines.push(...skills.slice(0, 8));\n   100→      if (skills.length > 8) lines.push(`  …and ${skills.length - > /Users/marvinrichter/Work/everything-claude-code/docs/system-review/components-2026-03-10/hooks.md << 'ENDOFFILE'\n# Hook System Audit — 2026-03-10\n\n## Summary\n\nTotal hook entries (in hooks.json): 19\nTotal hook scripts (scripts/hooks/*.js + external): 36 JS scripts + 1 shell script (observe.sh)\nReferenced scripts (from hooks.json): 15\nOverall system score: **7.6 / 10**\n\n---\n\n## Event Coverage Map\n\n| Event Type | Hook Count | Scripts Referenced |\n|---|---|---|\n| PreToolUse (Bash) | 1 | pre-bash-dispatch.js |\n| PreToolUse (Write) | 1 | doc-file-warning.js |\n| PreToolUse (Edit\\|Write) | 1 | suggest-compact.js (async) |\n| PreCompact (*) | 1 | pre-compact.js |\n| SessionStart (*) | 2 | session-start.js, context-banner.js |\n| PostToolUse (Agent) | 1 | agent-tracker.js (async) |\n| PostToolUse (Edit\\|Write) | 3 | auto-checkpoint.js, system-health-check.js, post-edit-workflow-nudge.js |\n| PostToolUse (Bash) | 2 | pr-url-logger.js, build-failure-router.js (async) |\n| PostToolUse (Edit) | 3 | post-edit-format-dispatch.js, post-edit-typecheck.js, post-edit-typecheck-rust.js |\n| PostToolUse (*) | 1 | observe.sh (async) |\n| Stop (*) | 1 | check-console-log.js |\n| SessionEnd (*) | 3 | session-end.js, evaluate-session.js, instinct-decay.js (async) |\n| Notification (*) | 1 | notification-handler.js |\n\n**Note:** `Stop` and `SessionEnd` are both present and cover different needs — `Stop` does the per-response console.log check, while `SessionEnd` does full session state persistence. This is intentional and correct.\n\n---\n\n## Dimension Scores\n\n| Dimension | Score | Weight | Weighted | Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| Event Coverage | 9 | 20% | 1.80 | All critical events covered including PreCompact, SessionStart, SessionEnd |\n| False Positive Risk | 7 | 15% | 1.05 | 2 broad-matcher concerns worth monitoring |\n| Performance Impact | 7 | 15% | 1.05 | post-edit-typecheck has 30s timeout; auto-checkpoint runs git on every Edit/Write |\n| Error Handling | 8 | 15% | 1.20 | Strong overall; observe.sh uses `set -e` without trap, one silent swallow |\n| Dead References | 8 | 10% | 0.80 | All 15 JS references exist; observe.sh exists; one config path discrepancy |\n| Dead Hooks | 9 | 10% | 0.90 | No dead hooks; all matchers map to plausible tool call paths |\n| Missing Critical Hooks | 8 | 10% | 0.80 | Two valuable gaps identified |\n| Interaction Conflicts | 7 | 5% | 0.35 | One structural conflict between auto-checkpoint and pre-bash-dispatch secret guard |\n\n**Overall: 7.95 / 10** (rounded to **8.0 / 10**)\n\n---\n\n## Detailed Findings by Dimension\n\n### 1. Event Coverage — Score 9\n\nAll six Claude Code hook events are covered:\n\n- `PreToolUse`: Bash safety + Write doc-warning + Edit|Write compact-suggestion\n- `PreCompact`: State snapshot before context summarization\n- `SessionStart`: Context injection, project detection, glob-rule matching, agent instincts\n- `PostToolUse`: Formatting, type-checking, checkpointing, nudges, agent tracking, build-routing\n- `Stop`: console.log scan after every response\n- `SessionEnd`: Session persistence, learning evaluation, instinct decay\n- `Notification`: Context pressure advisory + weekly digest\n\nThe `evaluate-session.js` is registered under `SessionEnd` even though its header comment says \"Stop hook\". This is a documentation inconsistency only — the hook is correctly placed in `SessionEnd` in hooks.json.\n\n### 2. False Positive Risk — Score 7\n\n**Concern 1 — PostToolUse `*` matcher (observe.sh)**\n\nThe wildcard `*` matcher on `PostToolUse` means `observe.sh` fires on every single tool call without exception — including Read, LS, Glob, Bash, Agent, TodoWrite, etc. Since `observe.sh` spawns two Python3 subprocesses per invocation, this is also a performance concern (see Dimension 3). The intent of broad observation is documented in the description, so this is intentional by design, but it adds noise to `observations.jsonl` with tool calls that carry no learning signal.\n\n**Concern 2 — post-edit-workflow-nudge: security-scan-nudge fires on path keywords**\n\nThe security nudge pattern (`SECURITY_KEYWORDS`) matches the file **path** (not content), testing for tokens like `auth`, `token`, `session`, `sign`, `verify`. This will fire on every edit to files named `session-end.js`, `pre-bash-dispatch.js`, `auth-utils.ts`, `sign-in-form.tsx` — none of which may have a security issue. The cooldown on `code-review-nudge` applies per hook-id, but `security-scan-nudge` has no cooldown, meaning it fires on every edit to these files.\n\n**Concern 3 — check-console-log (Stop event) scans all git-modified JS/TS files**\n\nThis fires after every Stop event and calls `git status --porcelain` + reads all modified JS/TS files. If a session modifies many files, this could read dozens of files. The exclusions for `scripts/` and test files are appropriate. Low false-positive risk, correctly excluded.\n\n### 3. Performance Impact — Score 7\n\n**post-edit-typecheck.js — HIGH LATENCY RISK**\n\nRuns `npx tsc --noEmit` synchronously (via `execFileSync`) with a **30-second timeout** on every `Edit` of a `.ts` or `.tsx` file. In a large TypeScript project, `tsc --noEmit` can take 10–30 seconds. This is a synchronous blocking call in a `PostToolUse` hook that is NOT marked `async: true`. Every TypeScript file edit will block Claude Code's next action for the duration of type checking.\n\nRecommendation: Either mark this hook `async: true` in hooks.json (currently absent for post-edit-typecheck), or increase the threshold and accept the tradeoff. Alternatively, use `tsc --noEmit --incremental` which is faster on subsequent runs.\n\n**post-edit-typecheck-rust.js — VERY HIGH LATENCY RISK**\n\nSame pattern as TypeScript checker, but runs `cargo check` with a **60-second timeout** synchronously. Rust compilation is notoriously slow on cold builds. This is also NOT marked `async: true` in hooks.json, so it blocks synchronously after every `.rs` file edit.\n\n**auto-checkpoint.js — MODERATE**\n\nRuns multiple `git` subprocesses (up to 4: `rev-parse`, `rev-parse HEAD`, `status --porcelain`, then `add -A` + `commit` or `stash`). The hook IS marked `async: true` with a 15-second timeout, which is correct. Rate-limited to 1 checkpoint per 60 seconds. Net impact is acceptable given the async flag.\n\n**observe.sh — MODERATE (frequency issue)**\n\nFires on every PostToolUse (`*` matcher). Spawns 2–3 Python3 subprocesses per call. Python startup overhead is ~50–100ms, so 2–3 subprocesses add ~100–300ms per tool call. The hook IS marked `async: true` with a 10-second timeout. This is the right choice given the frequency, but Python subprocess spawning on every tool call in a long session adds up.\n\n**post-edit-format-dispatch.js — ACCEPTABLE**\n\nUses `execFileSync` to call the language-specific formatter with a 5-second timeout. Formatters (biome, ruff, gofmt) are typically fast (<500ms). The 5-second timeout is appropriate. Not marked async, but formatters are fast enough that synchronous execution is acceptable.\n\n**Summary of blocking hooks:**\n\n| Hook | Event Frequency | Blocking? | Max Latency |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| post-edit-typecheck.js | Every .ts/.tsx Edit | YES | 30,000ms |\n| post-edit-typecheck-rust.js | Every .rs Edit | YES | 60,000ms |\n| post-edit-format-dispatch.js | Every Edit | YES | 5,000ms |\n| system-health-check.js | Every Edit\\|Write | YES | ~100ms (file I/O only) |\n| pre-bash-dispatch.js | Every Bash | YES | ~100ms + git diff (capped 5s) |\n\n### 4. Error Handling — Score 8\n\n**Strengths:**\n\n- All JS hooks use try/catch at the top level and exit with code 0 on errors — hooks never block Claude Code\n- `logHook()` from `hook-logger.js` wraps all writes in try/catch\n- `pre-bash-dispatch.js` has the only intentional blocking exit (code 2 for secret guard and dev server block), which is correct\n- Missing formatters are handled gracefully in `post-edit-format-dispatch.js` — clear error message with formatter name, exits 0\n- `session-end.js` and `session-start.js` have comprehensive error handling at each I/O operation\n\n**Issues:**\n\n**observe.sh uses `set -e` without an error trap (MEDIUM)**\n\n`set -e` causes the script to exit immediately if any command fails. If `python3` is not installed, `du -m` fails, or the `source detect-project.sh` fails, the script exits non-zero. Claude Code treats non-zero exit from an async hook as a warning, not a block — but the exit is silent (no user-facing message). The script should use `set -e` with `trap 'exit 0' ERR` to ensure it always exits cleanly, or remove `set -e` and handle errors explicitly.\n\n**evaluate-session.js reads a config path that does not match the installed location**\n\nThe script reads config from `skills/continuous-learning/config.json` (without `-v2`), but the hooks.json references `skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh`. If `continuous-learning/config.json` does not exist, the script falls back to defaults silently — this is handled gracefully. The path mismatch is a documentation/maintenance inconsistency but not a runtime error.\n\n**auto-checkpoint.js runs `git commit --no-verify`**\n\nThe checkpoint commit bypasses pre-commit hooks. This is intentional (checkpoints should not trigger the secret guard), but it means checkpoint commits bypass the pre-bash-dispatch.js secret guard. This is documented in the hook header. The tradeoff is acceptable since checkpoint commits are labeled `[skip ci]` and are never pushed directly.\n\n### 5. Dead References — Score 8\n\nAll 15 Node.js scripts referenced in hooks.json exist at their expected paths under `scripts/hooks/`. The external reference `${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/skills/continuous-learning-v2/hooks/observe.sh` exists. `${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/scripts/instinct-decay.js` exists.\n\n**One path discrepancy (LOW):**\n\n`evaluate-session.js` reads config from `skills/continuous-learning/config.json` (old path, pre-v2 naming), while the hook system was updated to reference `continuous-learning-v2`. If only `continuous-learning-v2/config.json` exists (not `continuous-learning/config.json`), the evaluator will silently use defaults. This is gracefully handled but creates a silent misconfiguration.\n\n**Scripts in scripts/hooks/ with no hooks.json reference (not dead references, but orphaned scripts):**\n\nThe following 21 scripts exist in `scripts/hooks/` but are NOT directly referenced in `hooks.json` — they are dispatched dynamically by `post-edit-format-dispatch.js`:\n`post-edit-format.js`, `post-edit-format-python.js`, `post-edit-format-go.js`, `post-edit-format-java.js`, `post-edit-format-swift.js`, `post-edit-format-rust.js`, `post-edit-format-cpp.js`, `post-edit-format-bash.js`, `post-edit-format-kotlin.js`, `post-edit-format-sql.js`, `post-edit-format-scala.js`, `post-edit-format-c.js`, `post-edit-format-php.js`, `post-edit-format-r.js`, `post-edit-format-csharp.js`, `post-edit-format-dart.js`, `hook-logger.js`.\n\nThese are correctly used as dispatch targets and library modules — they are not dead references.\n\n### 6. Dead Hooks — Score 9\n\nNo hooks are demonstrably dead. All matchers correspond to tools that Claude Code uses:\n\n- `Bash` — used constantly\n- `Write` / `Edit` — used on every file modification\n- `Edit|Write` — compound of the above\n- `Agent` — used when Claude invokes subagents\n- `*` (wildcard) — always fires\n\nThe `post-edit-typecheck-rust.js` and `post-edit-typecheck.js` hooks only perform real work when `.rs` or `.ts/.tsx` files are edited, respectively. In a non-Rust / non-TypeScript project they exit early at the file extension check — this is not a dead hook, just appropriately selective.\n\n### 7. Missing Critical Hooks — Score 8\n\n**Gap 1 — No PreToolUse hook for Write on binary or large files (MEDIUM)**\n\n`post-edit-format-dispatch.js` fires on all `Edit` events and dispatches by extension. It does not fire on `Write`. If Claude uses `Write` to create a new file (not edit an existing one), the formatter does NOT run. This is a known architectural gap: auto-formatting is Edit-only. New file creation via `Write` skips formatting. This affects all languages. A `PostToolUse Write` hook dispatching to `post-edit-format-dispatch.js` would close this gap.\n\n**Gap 2 — No PreToolUse hook for large Write operations (LOW)**\n\nThere is no guard that warns before writing very large files (e.g., accidentally writing a generated file or a binary blob). The doc-file-warning.js covers only `.md` and `.txt` — a general file-size pre-check for `Write` would prevent accidental large writes.\n\n**Gap 3 — No PreToolUse security scan on Edit content (MEDIUM)**\n\n`pre-bash-dispatch.js` scans staged git diffs for secrets before `git commit`. However, there is no PreToolUse hook that scans the `new_string` content of an `Edit` call before writing it to disk. Secrets could be written to files (not yet committed) without triggering the guard. The current guard catches secrets at commit time, which is correct but is a second-layer check. A PreToolUse Edit/Write content-scanner would catch secrets earlier.\n\n### 8. Interaction Conflicts — Score 7\n\n**Conflict 1 — auto-checkpoint creates commits that bypass pre-bash-dispatch.js secret guard (MEDIUM)**\n\n`auto-checkpoint.js` creates `git commit --no-verify` on every Edit/Write. These checkpoint commits bypass all pre-commit hooks, including the secret-guard pattern in `pre-bash-dispatch.js`. If Claude writes a file containing a secret and it is auto-checkpointed before `git commit` is run, the secret lands in git history. The user would need to specifically run `git commit` (without `--no-verify`) to trigger the guard — but checkpoint commits are always `--no-verify`.\n\nMitigation in place: checkpoint commits are labeled `[skip ci]` and auto-checkpoint's own rate limiting means not every file write becomes a checkpoint commit. However, secrets in checkpointed commits ARE in git history.\n\nRecommendation: Run the secret-scan pattern directly inside `auto-checkpoint.js` before creating the checkpoint commit, or switch the checkpoint strategy to `git stash` when the initial commit exists (matching the strategy used when no initial commit exists).\n\n**Conflict 2 — post-edit-format-dispatch.js + post-edit-typecheck.js both run on every .ts Edit (LOW)**\n\nBoth hooks fire synchronously on `.ts` file edits. Format dispatch runs first (5s timeout), typecheck second (30s timeout). If formatting changes the file on disk, the typecheck runs against the formatted version — this is actually the desired behavior. No real conflict, but cumulative latency on every `.ts` edit can reach 35 seconds in the worst case.\n\n**Conflict 3 — suggest-compact.js has a race condition on the counter file (LOW)**\n\n`suggest-compact.js` uses file-descriptor-based read-truncate-write to maintain a tool call counter. The comment acknowledges the race window between concurrent hook invocations. In practice, PreToolUse hooks run sequentially per tool call, so this should not be a real-world issue unless Claude Code parallelizes hook invocations.\n\n---\n\n## Issues Table\n\n| Severity | Dimension | Hook / Script | Finding | Suggestion |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| HIGH | Performance | post-edit-typecheck.js | `tsc --noEmit` runs synchronously (execFileSync) with 30s timeout on every .ts/.tsx Edit. Blocks Claude Code for the full type-check duration. | Add `\"async\": true` to the hooks.json entry for post-edit-typecheck, or switch to `tsc --noEmit --incremental` for faster subsequent runs. |\n| HIGH | Performance | post-edit-typecheck-rust.js | `cargo check` runs synchronously (execFileSync) with 60s timeout on every .rs Edit. Cold Rust builds can consume the full 60 seconds, blocking all subsequent tool calls. | Add `\"async\": true` to the hooks.json entry for post-edit-typecheck-rust. |\n| MEDIUM | Interaction Conflicts | auto-checkpoint.js | Checkpoint commits use `--no-verify`, bypassing the secret guard in `pre-bash-dispatch.js`. Secrets written by Claude to a file and auto-checkpointed will enter git history before any pre-commit secret scan. | Either run the secret-scan patterns inside `auto-checkpoint.js` before committing, or add a note in the commit message to warn users that checkpoint commits are not secret-scanned. |\n| MEDIUM | False Positive Risk | post-edit-workflow-nudge.js | `security-scan-nudge` matches the file **path** for security keywords (auth, token, session, etc.), not file content. Files like `session-end.js`, `auth-utils.ts`, or `sign-in-form.tsx` will trigger this nudge on every edit, regardless of whether any security-sensitive code was changed. No cooldown is applied to this nudge. | Apply the same cooldown mechanism used by `code-review-nudge` to `security-scan-nudge`, or scope the match to file content rather than (or in addition to) the file path. |\n| MEDIUM | Missing | post-edit-format-dispatch.js | Auto-formatting only fires on `Edit` events. Files created via `Write` (new file creation) are never formatted automatically. | Add a `PostToolUse Write` hook entry in hooks.json pointing to `post-edit-format-dispatch.js`, or extend the existing `Edit\\|Write` pattern for system-health-check to also cover the formatter. |\n| MEDIUM | Error Handling | observe.sh | `set -e` causes silent non-zero exit if `python3` is missing, `source detect-project.sh` fails, or `du -m` errors. The hook exits non-zero silently, which may surface as a warning in Claude Code logs but provides no diagnostic message. | Add `trap 'exit 0' ERR` immediately after `set -e`, or replace `set -e` with explicit per-command error handling. |\n| LOW | Dead References | evaluate-session.js | Reads config from `skills/continuous-learning/config.json` (original path), but the hook system was migrated to `continuous-learning-v2`. If only the v2 directory exists, config loading silently falls back to defaults. | Update the config path in `evaluate-session.js` to `skills/continuous-learning-v2/config.json`, or add a fallback that checks both paths. |\n| LOW | Performance | observe.sh | Spawns 2–3 Python3 subprocesses on every PostToolUse (`*` matcher). Python startup is ~50–100ms each. In sessions with many tool calls, this adds 100–300ms per call (async, so non-blocking). | Consider porting the JSON parsing and observation writing to a Node.js script, reducing subprocess overhead to a single Node.js process (already running for all other hooks). |\n| LOW | Interaction Conflicts | post-edit-typecheck.js + post-edit-format-dispatch.js | Both fire synchronously on .ts Edit. Combined worst-case blocking latency is 35 seconds per TypeScript file edit (5s format + 30s type-check). | Mark both as `async: true` to decouple them from Claude Code's response cycle. Warnings appear in stderr regardless of async mode. |\n\n---\n\n## Top 3 Missing Hook Opportunities\n\n### 1. PostToolUse Write — Auto-Format on New Files (Highest Value)\n\nEvery new file created by Claude via the `Write` tool is skipped by `post-edit-format-dispatch.js`. In practice, Claude creates many new files (new components, new modules, new test files) via `Write`, and all of them land on disk unformatted. This is the single highest-value missing hook because it affects the most common file-creation workflow.\n\n**Implementation:** Add to hooks.json `PostToolUse` section:\n```json\n{\n  \"matcher\": \"Write\",\n  \"hooks\": [\n    {\n      \"type\": \"command\",\n      \"command\": \"node \\\"${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/scripts/hooks/post-edit-format-dispatch.js\\\"\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"description\": \"Auto-format new files created via Write tool\"\n}\n```\n\nThe `post-edit-format-dispatch.js` script already reads `file_path` from `tool_input` — no script changes needed, only a hooks.json entry.\n\n### 2. PreToolUse Edit|Write — Content-Level Secret Scanner (Medium Value)\n\nThe current secret guard (`pre-bash-dispatch.js`) scans staged git diffs before `git commit`. This catches secrets at commit time. A PreToolUse guard on `Edit` and `Write` would catch secrets **before they are written to disk**, providing an earlier detection layer that is also immune to the `--no-verify` bypass in `auto-checkpoint.js`.\n\n**Implementation:** Extend `pre-bash-dispatch.js` logic into a new `pre-write-secret-guard.js` that reads `new_string` (for Edit) or `content` (for Write) from `tool_input` and runs the `SECRET_PATTERNS` scan.\n\n### 3. PostToolUse Bash — Test Runner Success/Failure Tracker (Lower Value)\n\n`build-failure-router.js` detects build/compile errors in Bash output. There is no complementary hook that captures test run results (pass/fail/coverage) from `pytest`, `jest`, `vitest`, `go test`, `cargo test` output. A lightweight test-result tracker could feed the `continuous-learning-v2` observation pipeline and surface test coverage trends without requiring manual inspection.\n\n---\n\n## Reliability Score\n\n```\nOverall system score: 7.6 / 10\n\nBreakdown:\n  Event Coverage     9.0 × 0.20 = 1.80\n  False Positive     7.0 × 0.15 = 1.05\n  Performance        7.0 × 0.15 = 1.05\n  Error Handling     8.0 × 0.15 = 1.20\n  Dead References    8.0 × 0.10 = 0.80\n  Dead Hooks         9.0 × 0.10 = 0.90\n  Missing Hooks      8.0 × 0.10 = 0.80\n  Conflicts          7.0 × 0.05 = 0.35\n  ─────────────────────────────────────\n  Total                          7.95\n```\n\nThe hook system is well-architected and production-capable. The two HIGH-severity issues (TypeScript and Rust type-checkers running synchronously) are the most impactful — fixing them requires only two lines in hooks.json (`\"async\": true`). The MEDIUM-severity auto-checkpoint/secret-guard conflict requires a code change in `auto-checkpoint.js`. All other issues are LOW severity or represent acceptable design tradeoffs.\n\nENDOFFILE\necho \"Written\"","description":"Write the full hook system audit report"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":"tool_use","stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":178,"cache_read_input_tokens":78085,"output_tokens":6206,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":178},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}},"requestId":"req_011CYtQu1bcwTc1M9YF3rmk3","type":"assistant","uuid":"a98e3e6e-2a9d-4829-8b57-1dee72dafa43","timestamp":"2026-03-09T23:59:59.410Z"}

\nScripts directly referenced in hooks.json: 15  \nOverall system score: **7.6 / 10**\n\n---\n\n## Event Coverage Map\n\n| Event Type | Hook Count | Scripts Referenced |\n|---|---|---|\n| PreToolUse (Bash) | 1 | pre-bash-dispatch.js |\n| PreToolUse (Write) | 1 | doc-file-warning.js |\n| PreToolUse (Edit\\|Write) | 1 | suggest-compact.js (async) |\n| PreCompact (*) | 1 | pre-compact.js |\n| SessionStart (*) | 2 | session-start.js, context-banner.js |\n| PostToolUse (Agent) | 1 | agent-tracker.js (async) |\n| PostToolUse (Edit\\|Write) | 3 | auto-checkpoint.js (async),
